click.echo(f\"📦 Installing skill '{skill_name}' to {target_path}...\")\n\n    success, message = install_skill_command(\n        skill_name=skill_name, target_path=target_path, force=force\n    )\n\n    if success:\n        click.echo(f\"✅ {message}\")\n    else:\n        click.echo(f\"❌ {message}\", err=True)\n        sys.exit(1)\n\n\n@main.command()\n@click.option(\n    \"--verbose\",\n    is_flag=True,\n    help=\"Show detailed diagnostic information\",\n)\ndef doctor(verbose: bool):\n    \"\"\"\n    Check SuperClaude installation health\n\n    Verifies:\n        - pytest plugin loaded correctly\n        - Skills installed (if any)\n        - Configuration files present\n    \"\"\"\n    from .doctor import run_doctor\n\n    click.echo(\"🔍 SuperClaude Doctor\\n\")\n\n    results = run_doctor(verbose=verbose)\n\n    # Display results\n    for check in results[\"checks\"]:\n        status_symbol = \"✅\" if check[\"passed\"] else \"❌\"\n        click.echo(f\"{status_symbol} {check['name']}\")\n\n        if verbose and check.get(\"details\"):\n            for detail in check[\"details\"]:\n                click.echo(f\"    {detail}\")\n\n    # Summary\n    click.echo()\n    total = len(results[\"checks\"])\n    passed = sum(1 for check in results[\"checks\"] if check[\"passed\"])\n\n    if passed == total:\n        click.echo(\"✅ SuperClaude is healthy\")\n    else:\n        click.echo(f\"⚠️  {total - passed}/{total} checks failed\")\n        sys.exit(1)\n\n\n@main.command()\ndef version():\n    \"\"\"Show SuperClaude version\"\"\"\n    click.echo(f\"SuperClaude version {__version__}\")\n\n\nfrom superclaude.cli.sprint import sprint_group\n\nmain.add_command(sprint_group, name=\"sprint\")\n\nfrom superclaude.cli.roadmap import roadmap_group\n\nmain.add_command(roadmap_group, name=\"roadmap\")\n\nfrom superclaude.cli.cleanup_audit import cleanup_audit_group\n\nmain.add_command(cleanup_audit_group, cli_portify_group\n\nmain.add_command(cli_portify_group)\n\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()\n```\n\n## 2. How `main.py` registers subcommands\n\nThe existing pattern is:\n\n```python\nfrom superclaude.cli.sprint import sprint_group\nmain.add_command(sprint_group, name=\"sprint\")\n\nfrom superclaude.cli.roadmap import roadmap_group\nmain.add_command(roadmap_group, name=\"roadmap\")\n\nfrom superclaude.cli.cleanup_audit import cleanup_audit_group\nmain.add_command(cleanup_audit_group, name=\"cleanup-audit\")\n\nfrom superclaude.cli.tasklist import tasklist_group\nmain.add_command(tasklist_group, name=\"tasklist\")\n\nfrom superclaude.cli.cli_portify.commands import cli_portify_group\nmain.add_command(cli_portify_group)\n```\n\nPattern notes:\n\n- Group objects are imported near the bottom of `main.py`.\n- Most are registered with explicit CLI name strings.\n- `cli_portify_group` is registered without an explicit `name=...`, so it relies on the group’s own declared name.\n- There is currently no analogous import/add for `prd`.\n\n## 3. `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/sprint/commands.py`\n\nVerbatim full file:\n\n```python\n\"\"\"Sprint CLI commands — Click command group and subcommands.\n\nDefines the \"--model\",\n    default=\"\",\n    help=\"Claude model to use (default: env CLAUDE_MODEL or claude default)\",\n)\n@click.option(\n    \"--dry-run\",\n    is_flag=True,\n    help=\"Show discovered phases without executing\",\n)\n@click.option(\n    \"--no-tmux\",\n    is_flag=True,\n    help=\"Run in foreground even if tmux is available\",\n)\n@click.option(\n    \"--permission-flag\",\n \"--stall-timeout\",\n    type=int,\n    default=0,\n    help=\"Stall timeout in seconds (0 = disabled, default: 0)\",\n)\n@click.option(\n    \"--stall-action\",\n    type=click.Choice([\"warn\", `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/prd/config.py`\n\n```python\n\"\"\"PRD pipeline configuration -- CLI argument resolution and PrdConfig construction.\n\nResolves CLI arguments into a fully-populated ``PrdConfig`` instance with\nsensible defaults, path resolution, and tier validation.\n\nNFR-PRD.1: Zero ``async def`` or ``await`` in this module.\nNFR-PRD.7: No imports from superclaude.cli.sprint or superclaude.cli.roadmap.\n\"\"\"\n\nfrom __future__ import annotations\n\nimport re\nfrom pathlib import Path\nfrom typing import Optional, Sequence\n\nfrom superclaude.cli.prd.models import PrdConfig\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# Constants\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n_VALID_TIERS = frozenset({\"lightweight\", \"standard\", \"heavyweight\"})\n\n# Known step ID patterns for resume validation.\n# Step IDs follow the pattern: word-word or word-word-word (kebab-case).\n_STEP_ID_PATTERN = re.compile(\n    r\"^(check-existing|parse-request|scope-discovery|research-notes\"\n    r\"|sufficiency-review|template-triage|build-task-file|verify-task-file\"\n    r\"|preparation|investigation-\\d+|web-research-\\d+\"\n    r\"|analyst-completeness|qa-research-gate\"\n    r\"|synthesis-\\d+|analyst-synthesis|qa-synthesis-gate\"\n    r\"|assembly|structural-qa|qualitative-qa|completion)$\"\n)\n\n_DEFAULT_SKILL_REFS_DIRS = [\n    Path(\"src/superclaude/skills/prd/refs\"),\n    Path(\".claude/skills/prd/refs\"),\n]\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# Public API\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\ndef resolve_config(\n    request: str,\n    *,\n    product: Optional[str] = None,\n    where: Optional[Sequence[str]] = None,\n    output: Optional[str] = None,\n    tier: Optional[str] = None,\n    max_turns: Optional[int] = None,\n    model: Optional[str] = None,\n    dry_run: bool = False,\n    debug: bool = False,\n    resume_from: Optional[str] = None,\n) -> PrdConfig:\n    \"\"\"Resolve CLI arguments into a fully-populated ``PrdConfig``.\n\n    Args:\n        request: Natural-language product request (positional CLI arg).\n        product: Product name or scope override.\n        where: Source directories to focus on.\n        output: Output path for final PRD (defaults to \".\").\n        tier: Pipeline tier -- must be one of \"lightweight\", \"standard\",\n              \"heavyweight\". Defaults to \"standard\".\n        max_turns: Turn budget for subprocesses. Defaults to 300.\n        model: Claude model to use.\n        dry_run: Validate config without executing.\n        debug: Enable debug logging.\n        resume_from: Step ID to resume from (validates format).\n\n    Returns:\n        A validated ``PrdConfig`` ready for pipeline execution.\n\n    Raises:\n        ValueError: If *tier* is invalid or *resume_from* has an\n            unrecognised format.\n    \"\"\"\n    # -- Tier validation --\n    resolved_tier = (tier or \"standard\").lower().strip()\n    if resolved_tier not in _VALID_TIERS:\n        raise ValueError(\n            f\"Invalid tier {resolved_tier!r}. \"\n            f\"Must be one of: {', '.join(sorted(_VALID_TIERS))}\"\n        )\n\n    # -- Resume validation --\n    if resume_from is not None:\n        resume_from = resume_from.strip()\n        if not _STEP_ID_PATTERN.match(resume_from):\n            raise ValueError(\n                f\"Unrecognised resume step ID: {resume_from!r}. \"\n                f\"Expected a known step pattern like 'parse-request', \"\n                f\"'investigation-3', 'qa-synthesis-gate', etc.\"\n            )\n\n    # -- Path resolution --\n    output_path = Path(output).resolve() if output else Path(\".\").resolve()\n\n    # Derive product slug from product name or request\n    product_name = product or \"\"\n    product_slug = _slugify(product_name) if product_name else \"\"\n\n    # Task directory: derived from output_path + product_slug (or 'prd-task')\n    task_dir_name = f\"prd-{product_slug}\" if product_slug else \"prd-task\"\n    task_dir = output_path / task_dir_name\n\n    # Skill refs directory: auto-discover from known locations\n    skill_refs_dir = _discover_skill_refs_dir()\n\n    return PrdConfig(\n        user_message=request,\n        product_name=product_name,\n        product_slug=product_slug,\n        where=list(where) if where else [],\n        output_path=output_path,\n        tier=resolved_tier,\n        task_dir=task_dir,\n        skill_refs_dir=skill_refs_dir,\n        max_turns=max_turns or 300,\n        model=model or \"\",\n        dry_run=dry_run,\n        debug=debug,\n        resume_from=resume_from,\n    )\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# Internal Helpers\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\ndef _slugify(name: str) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Convert a product name to a kebab-case slug.\"\"\"\n    slug = name.lower().strip()\n    slug = re.sub(r\"[^a-z0-9]+\", \"-\", slug)\n    return slug.strip(\"-\")\n\n\ndef _discover_skill_refs_dir() -> Path:\n    \"\"\"Find the skill refs directory from known locations.\n\n    Returns the first existing directory, or the default if none found.\n    \"\"\"\n    for candidate in _DEFAULT_SKILL_REFS_DIRS:\n        if candidate.is_dir():\n            return candidate\n    # Fallback to the canonical source location even if it doesn't exist yet\n    return _DEFAULT_SKILL_REFS_DIRS[0]\n```\n\n### `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/prd/diagnostics.py`\n\n```python\n\"\"\"PRD pipeline diagnostics -- failure classification, collection, and reporting.\n\nProvides post-failure analysis by collecting step results, gate failures,\nand fix cycle history into a structured diagnostic report. The failure\nclassifier assigns a category based on PrdStepStatus values.\n\nNFR-PRD.1: Zero ``async def`` or ``await`` in this module.\nNFR-PRD.6/GAP-007: Resume command generation with step-level and\n    per-agent granularity.\nNFR-PRD.7: No imports from superclaude.cli.sprint or superclaude.cli.roadmap.\n\"\"\"\n\nfrom __future__ import annotations\n\nfrom dataclasses import dataclass, ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# Failure categories\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\nclass PrdFailureCategory(Enum):\n    \"\"\"Classification of PRD pipeline step failure root cause.\"\"\"\n\n    TIMEOUT = \"timeout\"\n    QA_FAIL = \"qa_fail\"\n    BUDGET_EXHAUSTED = overall_status: str = \"success\"\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# DiagnosticCollector\n# self._step_results.append(result)\n\n    def record_gate_failure(\n        self, step_id: str, reason: str, enforcement: str\n    ) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Record a gate failure.\"\"\"\n        self._gate_failures.append({\n            \"step_id\": step_id,\n            \"reason\": reason,\n            \"enforcement\": enforcement,\n        })\n\n    def record_fix_cycle(\n        self,\n        step_id: str,\n        cycle_number: int,\n        verdict: str,\n        agent_id: str = \"\",\n    ) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Record a fix cycle attempt.\"\"\"\n    def build_report(\n        self, pipeline_result: PrdPipelineResult\n    ) -> PrdDiagnosticReport:\n        \"\"\"Build the complete diagnostic report.\"\"\"\n        report =      )\n        report.steps_failed = sum(\n            1 for r in self._step_results if r.status.is_failure\n        )\n        report.steps_skipped = sum(\n            1\n            for r in       \"fix_cycle\": r.fix_cycle,\n            }\n            for r in self._step_results\n            if r.status.is_failure\n        ]\n\n        report.gate_failures = list(self._gate_failures)\n        report.fix_cycle_history = list(self._fix_cycle_history)\n        report.resume_command = pipeline_result.resume_command()\n        report.overall_status = pipeline_result.outcome\n\n        return report\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# FailureClassifier\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\nclass FailureClassifier:\n    \"\"\"Maps PrdStepStatus values to user-facing failure categories.\"\"\"\n\n    def classify(self, result: PrdStepResult) -> PrdFailureCategory:\n        \"\"\"Determine the failure category for a step result.\n\n        Classification priority:\n        1. TIMEOUT: Step timed out\n        2. QA_FAIL: QA check returned FAIL\n        3. BUDGET_EXHAUSTED: Fix cycles exhausted\n        4. GATE_FAIL: Gate validation failed\n        5. CRASH: Unexpected non-zero exit\n        6. UNKNOWN: No clear evidence\n        \"\"\"\n        status = result.status\n\n        if status == PrdStepStatus.TIMEOUT:\n            return PrdFailureCategory.TIMEOUT\n\n        if status == PrdStepStatus.QA_FAIL:\n            return PrdFailureCategory.QA_FAIL\n\n        if status == PrdStepStatus.QA_FAIL_EXHAUSTED:\n            return PrdFailureCategory.BUDGET_EXHAUSTED\n\n        if status == PrdStepStatus.VALIDATION_FAIL:\n            return PrdFailureCategory.GATE_FAIL\n\n        if status == PrdStepStatus.ERROR:\n            return PrdFailureCategory.CRASH\n\n        if status == PrdStepStatus.HALT:\n            # HALT could be gate failure or crash depending on context\n            if result.gate_failure_reason:\n                return PrdFailureCategory.GATE_FAIL\n            return PrdFailureCategory.CRASH\n\n        return PrdFailureCategory.UNKNOWN\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# ReportGenerator\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\nclass ReportGenerator:\n    \"\"\"Generates human-readable diagnostic reports with resume commands.\"\"\"\n\n    def generate(self, report: PrdDiagnosticReport) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Produce a diagnostic summary as markdown.\"\"\"\n        lines = [\n            \"# PRD Pipeline Diagnostic Report\",\n            \"\",\n            \"## Summary\",\n            f\"- **Status**: {report.overall_status}\",\n            f\"- **Total Steps**: {report.total_steps}\",\n            f\"- **Passed**: detail.get(\"status\", \"unknown\")\n                exit_code = detail.get(\"exit_code\", -1)\n                agent = detail.get(\"agent_type\", \"\")\n                cycle = detail.get(\"fix_cycle\", 0)\n                lines.append(\n                    f\"- **{step}**: {status} (exit={exit_code}\"\n                    f\"{f', agent={agent}' if agent else ''}\"\n                    f\"{f', cycle={cycle}' if cycle else ''})\"\n                )\n\n        if report.gate_failures:\n            lines.append(\"\")\n            lines.append(\"## Gate Failures\")\n            for gf in report.gate_failures:\n                lines.append(\n                    f\"- **{gf['step_id']}** [{gf['enforcement']}]: \"\n                    f\"{gf['reason']}\"\n                )\n\n        if report.fix_cycle_history:\n            lines.append(\"\")\n            lines.append(\"## Fix Cycle History\")\n            for fc in report.fix_cycle_history:\n                agent_info = f\" (agent: {fc['agent_id']})\" if fc.get(\"agent_id\") else \"\"\n                lines.append(\n                    f\"- **{fc['step_id']}** cycle {fc['cycle_number']}: \"\n                    f\"{fc['verdict']}{agent_info}\"\n                )\n\n        if report.resume_command:\n            lines.append(\"\")\n            lines.append(\"## Resume\")\n            lines.append(f\"```\\n{report.resume_command}\\n```\")\n            suggested_budget = report.config.max_turns\n            lines.append(f\"Suggested budget: {suggested_budget} turns\")\n\n        return \"\\n\".join(lines)\n\n    def generate_resume_command(\n        self,\n        pipeline_result: PrdPipelineResult,\n        *,\n        failed_agent_id: str = \"\",\n    ) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Generate a CLI resume command for mid-run failures.\n\n        NFR-PRD.6/GAP-007: Step-level and per-agent granularity.\n\n        Args:\n            pipeline_result: The pipeline result with halt info.\n            failed_agent_id: If the failure occurred in a parallel group,\n                the specific agent that failed (GAP-007).\n\n        Returns:\n            CLI command string for resuming the pipeline.\n        \"\"\"\n        cmd = pipeline_result.resume_command()\n        if not cmd:\n            return \"\"\n\n        # Add per-agent resume hint for parallel group failures\n        if failed_agent_id:\n            cmd += f\" --agent {failed_agent_id}\"\n\n        # Add budget suggestion\n        budget = pipeline_result.suggested_resume_budget\n        cmd += f\" --max-turns {budget}\"\n\n        return cmd\n```\n\n### `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/prd/filtering.py`\n\n```python\n\"\"\"PRD pipeline filtering -- partitioning, ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\ndef partition_files(\n    files: list, threshold: int\n) -> list[list]:\n    \"\"\"Split a file list into partitions for parallel processing.\n\n    If the file count is at or below the threshold, returns a single\n    partition containing all files. Above the threshold, splits into\n    roughly even partitions where each partition has at most ``threshold``\n    items.\n\n    Args:\n        files: List of file paths (or any items) to partition.\n        threshold: Maximum items per partition.\n\n    Returns:\n        A list of partitions (each partition is a list of items).\n        Returns an empty list if files is empty.\n    \"\"\"\n    if not files:\n        return []\n    if len(files) <= threshold:\n        return [list(files)]\n\n    num_partitions = math.ceil(len(files) / threshold)\n    partition_size = math.ceil(len(files) / num_partitions)\n\n    partitions: list[list] = []\n    for i in range(0, len(files), partition_size):\n        partitions.append(list(files[i : i + partition_size]))\n    return partitions\n\n\n#
